. predictms, transmatrix(mat_five_states) models(m2_1_ggam m2_2_ggam m2_3_logn m2_4_logn) ///
>          timevar(timevar0) /// mint(0) maxt(1096) timevar() cannot be specified with mint()/maxt()/obs()
>          seed(2125) n(100) los diff ratio /// * si agrego bootstrap, at#() limit reached, or unrecognised option
>          from(1) ci reset bootstrap m(50)   /// * es una forma de hacer bootstrap 
>          at1(tipo_de_plan_res_1 0 TD_1 1 TD_2 0 TD_3 0 TD_4 0 _start 0) at2(tipo_de_plan_res_1 1 TD_1 1 TD_2 0 TD_3 0 TD_4 0 _start 0)

  2.         scalar variable = "`var'"
  3.         levelsof `var' if inrange(timevar01, .32, .34)|inrange(timevar01, .999, 1.02)|inrange(timevar01, 2.99, 3.02)|inrange(timevar01, 4.999, 5.02), local(mylevs) sep(,)
  4. 
.                                         tokenize "`mylevs'", parse(" ,") // `1', `2', ... will hold the elements of the big macro  "`local(mylevs)'"
  5.                                         local done = 0
  6.                                         local i = 0
  7.                                         local count = 0
  8.                                         while !`done' {  
  9.                                            local ++i
 10.                                                 local next = "``i''"
 11.                                                 local done = ("`next'" == "")
 12.                                            // Include elements that are not the parsing character itself.
.                                                  if ("`next'" != ",") & (!`done') {
 13.                                                    local ++count
 14.                                                    scalar est_n`count' = "`next'"
 15.                                                 }  
 16.                                         }
 17.                                         //
.                                         di "`count' est"
 18.                                         forval i = 1/`count' {
 19.                                           scalar est_n`i' = round(round(`=scalar(est_n`i')',.001)*100,.1)       
 20.                                           *scalar est_n`i' = "`=scalar(est_n`i')'"
.                                           di "`=scalar(est_n`i')'"
 21.                                         }       
 22.  di "`=scalar(variable)'"
 23.  di "`=scalar(est_n1)'"
